<script type='text/javascript'>
    jQuery(document).ready(function () {
        var portalNavi = jQuery(".portal-navi");
        var portalNaviLink = portalNavi.find(".icon_portal_navi");
        
        portalNaviLink.on("click", function (e) {
            portalNavi.toggleClass("active");
            e.stopPropagation();
            e.preventDefault();
        });
        jQuery(".login-dropdown-list a").on("click", function () {
            jQuery('#display-loader').removeClass("loader-display-none");
        });
        function hidePortalPanel() {
            var portalNaviElement = portalNavi.find(".cross-portal-navigation");
            if (jQuery(e.target).closest(portalNaviElement).length === 0) {
                portalNavi.removeClass("active");
            }
        }
        jQuery(document).on("click", function (e) {
            hidePortalPanel();
        }).on("keydown", function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode === 27) {
                hidePortalPanel();
            }
        });
    });

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

var uAgentText = window.navigator.userAgent;
if(uAgentText.indexOf("Safari")>0 && uAgentText.indexOf("Chrome")<0)
{
	var eleComTab = document.getElementById("MylistTab");
	if(eleComTab)
		eleComTab.style.padding="5px 12px 5px 12px";
}
function ChangeAlterLabelText(instrType)
{
    var lblText='group';
   if(instrType=='G')   
    lblText='group';
    else if(instrType=='F')
    lblText='fund';
    else if(instrType=='P')
    lblText='manager';    
    $('lbAlertText').innerHTML='Add a new '+lblText+' to your alerts';
}

    });
});
</script>

    <script type='text/javascript'>
        //googletag.pubads().refresh([unit5_sticky]); // If we need to refresh the ad slot we need to pass unit5_sticky variable from AdScript.js
        //IsAdsGeneratedUnit5 = false;

        var IsAdsGeneratedUnit5 = true;
        var IsUnit5_stickyDivCreated = false;

        jQuery(document).ready(function () {
            if (checkVisible(jQuery('#dynamicUnit5_stickySlot'))) {
                if (IsAdsGeneratedUnit4) {
                    if (!IsUnit5_stickyDivCreated) {
                        jQuery('#dynamicUnit5_stickySlot').append('<div id="Unit5_sticky" style="margin: 15px 0px;"></div>');
                        IsUnit5_stickyDivCreated = true;
                        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                            googletag.display('Unit5_sticky');
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        });

        jQuery(window).on('scroll',
            function() {
                if (checkVisible(jQuery('#dynamicUnit5_stickySlot'))) {
                    if (IsAdsGeneratedUnit5) {
                        if (!IsUnit5_stickyDivCreated) {
                            jQuery('#dynamicUnit5_stickySlot').append('<div id="Unit5_sticky" style="margin: 15px 0px;"></div>');
                            IsUnit5_stickyDivCreated = true;
                            googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                                googletag.display('Unit5_sticky');
                            });
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    IsAdsGeneratedUnit5 = true;
                }
            });
    </script>

    $('wholeCover').style.height = document.documentElement.scrollHeight.toString() + "px";

    if (GetCookie("uflag").length == 0) {
        SetCookie('utype', '');
        SetCookie('uflag', 'yes', 5000);
    }
    if (document.URL.toString().toLowerCase().indexOf("nonprivateinvestors.aspx") < 0) {
        if (GetCookie("utype") != 'PI' && !(GetCookie("utype") == '4' || GetCookie("utype") == '5') && GetCookie("Invest_UserId").length == 0) {
            $('UtypeLoginPopup').style.visibility = "hidden";
            $('UtypeNotLoginPopup').style.visibility = "visible";
        } else if (GetCookie("utype") != 'PI' && !(GetCookie("utype") == '4' || GetCookie("utype") == '5') && GetCookie("Invest_UserId").length > 0) {
            $('UtypeNotLoginPopup').style.visibility = "hidden";
            $('UtypeLoginPopup').style.visibility = "visible";
        }
    }

    function UtypePopupRedirect() {
        location.href = "/NonPrivateInvestors.aspx";
    }
    function NonLoginPrivateUser() {
        SetCookie('utype', 'PI', 30);
        $('UtypeNotLoginPopup').style.visibility = "hidden";
        $('UtypeLoginPopup').style.visibility = "hidden";
    }

    function LoginPrivateUser() {
        $('hdnPIUserType').value = '5';
        SetCookie('utype', 'PI', 30);
        document.mainForm.submit();
    }
    function setUser(ut) {
        SetCookie('utype',ut,30);
        $("selfCheck").style.visibility = "hidden";
        $("wholeCover").className = "wholeCoverHide";
        return void(0);
    }


</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function ResizePage() {
        if ($("mainBlock")) {
            $("mainForm").style.width = "985px";
            $("mainForm").style.margin = "auto";
            $("mainBlock").style.width = "960px";
        }
    }

    ResizePage();
    var attempts = 0, setTimeoutVar;
    function MoveAllAds() {
        //moveAdToPositionX("Top");
        moveAdToPositionX("TopRight");
        var topPos = jQuery('#dvTopRightAdContainer').offset().top + jQuery('#dvTopRightAdContainer').height() - jQuery('#content').offset().top +10+ 'px';
        jQuery('#bottomContainer').css('margin-top', topPos);
        attempts++;
        //console.log(attempts); // This log I kept for testing purpose only, Now Changes working fine hence commenting.
        if (attempts >= 3)
            window.clearInterval(setTimeoutVar);
    }
    window.onload = function() {
        setTimeoutVar = setInterval(MoveAllAds, 1000);
    };
    window.onresize = function() {
        setTimeoutVar = setInterval(MoveAllAds, 1000);
    };
    //window.onload = MoveAllAds;
    //window.onresize = MoveAllAds;
</script>
